Cut out the boring part, leave the good part.

  • For those familiar with the original Simon Sends manual. This sheet skips the letter counting step.
  • Top left cell is red letter. Row is the green letter. Column is the blue letter.
  • In each cell, the three letters in order are red, green, blue.
